	- I’ve seen some good ideas for a business so far. The thing is, everybody seems to be forgetting that B&D isn’t just a business.Was it you would have sold it when you got that proposition you told us about, and then would just have started something else.B&D has become a part of yourself.Thus, many of the ideas given so far, though could make you some money fast, wouldn’t follow the B&D mission and core idea, which is not to simply make money, but to offer great value (which far surpass the price that is being charged) and help men that are willing to do whatever it takes to excel and succeed.I’ve not read all the comments, but from the first ones I could only glimpse one that said something close to what I’ll suggest to you: the one about building the BAD Academy.The execution must be different than what was stated over there, though.I don’t see you making money from it by charging the rent from the people over there.The Academy, I believe, could be of tremendous help to both parties. To you and the lads that come seeking guidance.You would profit by having men with the mindset and will to build the empire your are looking into forging.They would profit by having a mentor to model themselves by and an environment where they could not just learn the right mindset and tools to kick some ass, but where they would be putting those tools and mindset into use, and by being surrounded by others with the same mentality and attitude. If they get nothing else from this program (which I doubt), this alone would already be worth gold for them and I’m certain would change the lives from all that could grasp this opportunity (I wish I could have had this kind of opportunity when I was 20. I would have developed then the mindset that only now I’m beginning to forge).So, summarizing: you would gain by having the right men to execute your plans of world domination, and they by having the opportunity to witness and learn what most modern men die without seeing and learning.A golden opportunity for both, I believe.The way to execute this idea would be completely up to you, since you’ll be bearing all the risks (but in the end will be reaping most of the rewards too).Some of the things to scrutinize before executing this idea would be:– The selection of the candidates. The moment you offer your readers the possibility of going through this apprenticeship you can be sure to have 50 times more responses than the number of comments in this post, as the potential rewards will far surpass the ones here.How will you identify the right ones to go through this process? How can you make sure that they already possess the right instincts and will to thrive through the program? Tough, but not impossible to find the right way to do it.– How long will the program last before the candidates are sent to do their killing on their own? I believe it would make a good (and healthy) policy to set them free after a while. There’s only so much you can learn and grow before you find yourself having to do all the calls and having to bear all the risks (or rewards, once you succeed) involved in the decision making process.It could be possible to offer them the possibility of continuing on the boat and help with world conquest. Not everyone wants to be rich anyway. And the atmosphere of a community as this can be hard to find. Personally, I’m not aware of any like this.– And how will the process itself be designed? Will there be a quarantine period where you’ll see if the candidates are made of clay or steel? Will they learn as they work or will both these processes be separated?Again, I have my own thoughts on this, but as this idea is already getting too long, and as there are a million different ways of doing it, but in the end you’ll be responsible for making the call, I’ll stop at what I’ve said so far.Of course you won’t make money as fast with this idea as with others, but unlike the others, once this project take off it will grow exponentially and eventually all you’ll have to do will be supervising the quality of your projects and brainstorming new ways of dominating the world, as at this point will already have a well structured army of Spartans ready to do some killing and ass kicking.I don’t know about you, my friend, but I’ve read a lot about the Spartans and sure as he’ll I’d like to see it reborn and taking on the world once again. If you don’t do it you can be sure that I will.Build the greatest project of all: build a community.Be the Lycurgus of the modern age.Good luck and Godspeed.(Sorry for any errors. 	- You can have a 60 second message or thoughtful tip recorded by you, or you could simply write down 60 words or less and send it to a good voice artist on Fiverr for only $5.00 dollars.
	- Then you can have your assistant update the voicemail whenever you want to change it.
	- The beauty of this, is that it costs you very little, but offers a lot of value. You do not have to update it everyday either. Just when you want.
	- People can call and plug into your motivational tip or thought of the day, week, month, etc.
	- Once you have a small collection of these quick advice tips, you can sell them as an audio download through your website and through CD Baby, creating more residual income for you, in small incremental ways.
	- I would love to pay $9.99 on Google Play or iTunes for a month’s worth of tips or something on a specific topic or what have you.
	- You could even offer the previous monthly audio tips in a downloadable format, in a subscription service for $2.99, $4.99 or $9.99 a month depending on how many times you want to create them.
	- You could write your tips in advance and not think about them all year.
	- If you wrote 36, sixty words or less tips, you could release just one a week for the whole year, while creating little motivaional audio books or rants, tips, whatever you want to call them, and sell them to those who want to buy them.
	- Hope this idea helps you.
	- Respectfully,
	- Alexander

The Genius of Simplicity can be applied to anything from cars, homes, brands, your own persona to even a blog. You see where Im going with this? Besides the fact that your page is already good as is, you can go that extra mile, well because I sence that you are as ambitious as I am. I hope one day I make it into the big leagues like you. First I need a good laptop, and if i win that first price thats what I would get.By the way I saw your workplace office, that room has the genius of Simplicity written all over. The first thing I thought was so fresh so clean, wow..I also read about your apprentice… what a privilege to work side by side with a mentor like Victor Pride. If you offered me an opportunity like that I would do it in a heartbeat.Hope my idea was helpful, and if I win I can go even further as to how we can apply to your successful blog without losing its kick ass edge.Everything happens for a reasonIMAGINATION IS THE LIMITyour friendJ-maci

		- Ryan says
	- April 24, 2015 at 3:47 am
	- Victor,
	- You should look into making what are called “Charitable Contribution Deductions”. In short, making “Charitable Contributions” to certain registered groups under certain guidelines can open you up for massive tax deductions, tax deductions at FAR greater rates than the charitable contribution you made. Most legitimate corporations do this and make lots of money from it. As long as your a corporation, it works. There are certain guidelines that I will post below. With that being said I’m not entirely sure where your website is based out of, or who you pay taxes to, but it’s worth looking into even if your based out of Vietnam and seeing if they have a similar set up.
	- http://www.irs.gov/Charities-&-Non-Profits/Charitable-Organizations/Charitable-Contribution-Deductions
	- http://www.irs.gov/uac/Eight-Tips-for-Deducting-Charitable-Contributions

		- HariDada says
	- April 24, 2015 at 12:07 pm
	- Hello Victor Pride,
	- My idea is related to 30 Days of Discipline and Body of a Spartan.
	- I see that you are selling the 30 Days of Discipline and the accountability workbook for $10 and Body of a Spartan + a free gift for $20.
	- Instead of selling your books, you can do a giveaway. See the example site mentioned below.
	- Example for 30 Days of Discipline (which can be easily cloned to Body of a Spartan as well):
	- I have setup a sample site here: http://bookgiveaways.net46.net/ (Giving away the pdf version of Think and Grow Rich – 260 pages)
	- (Instead of Think and Grow Rich, you can consider it as 30DOD / BOAS.)
	- This took me about 30 mins tops to put it up. Alright, the above site is an example of what I call a viral script.
	- Let me explain how the script works so you get an idea of how viral your site can become.
	- If you go down a bit on the example site, you can see the number of clicks and number of freebies table, 1 = 1, 5 = 2 and so on till 50 = 10
	- Whenever a new visitor comes to the site, a unique link “Your Special Link” is generated for them.
	- So, they have to post their unique link to get more traffic. Now the above table comes into effect.
	- When the above user sends one person to his link, the first “Not Available Yet” box opens which is a link to download a set of chapters from the Think and Grow Rich
	- book (Pages 1 – 52). Now, when the same person sends 5 more people, the second “Not Available Yet” box opens which is a link to download another set of chapters from
	- the Think and Grow Rich book (pages 53 – 78).
	- Similarly, when the same person sends
	- 10 people – 3rd link opens – download pages 79 to 10515 people – 4th link opens – download pages 106 to 14820 people – 5th link opens – download pages 149 to 17525 people – 6th link opens – download pages 176 to 20330 people – 7th link opens – download pages 204 to 21135 people – 8th link opens – download pages 212 to 21740 people – 9th link opens – download pages 218 to 22750 people – 10th link opens – download pages 228 to 260
	- So, for the first person to download all the chapters, he has to send 50 people and the viral effect continues…
	- Now, in the Let’s get started section, you can add certain rules like following you in twitter or whatever else. Or you can configure the first “Not Availabe yet” box
	- to link to your newsletter subscription page.
	- By adding the above script, you not only increase your site’s traffic, but can also increase your newsletter subscribers, twitter followers and earn more money too in
	- the process.
	- Monetization: All the above links can be monetized by content locking.
	- Script Requirements: A VPS / Dedi with lots of ram and bandwidth for the viral script to perform optimally.
	- This is just for 30DOD.
	- Have another VPS / Dedi for BOAS and you’re gonna make a killing!!!
	- PS: Lets do a JV instead of me giving you the script.
	- Yours Truly,
	- HariDada

		- Sven says
	- April 24, 2015 at 5:31 pm
	- Hi Vic,
	- I hope that my english is well enough.
	- Essentially you put the ideas in your own text, My twist on that idea is just following that train of thought to a certain end.
	- Let me get there:
	- – You have a bussiness, that brings in revenue– You want to increase that revenue– You do not want to be persoanlly involved in that process– There is a demand out there (probably in a lot of different countrys) beyond your blog for a personal interaction– So, like the realtor in your text should have done, you might consider sub-contracting.
	- Let me explain.
	- Many well know Workout systems or Self Defense systems were thought up by one guy. That one guy does not teach each and every class of that system but a “certified trainer” (sometimes there are even several levels). Sometimes this “inventor” does a very rare (and expensive) personal appearance, but most of the times, just interacts via his blog
	- First – people will pay you, to become one of this “trainers”. You would have to do very few things, if any, personally, This might even be an online course …Second – This trainers will give seminars, courses… based on your “system”. Part of that income created that way goes to you.Third – These trainers will train others (to a certain extent) and by doing this, your income will increase once again.
	- The important part would be to limit the number of this trainers and have a good system for picking the right guys and training them. But actually you would just need one person to oversee that process…
